<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Our ability to achieve identical supermarket
sales and earnings growth and earnings per share goals may be affected by:
labor disputes, particularly as the Company seeks to manage health care and
pension costs; industry consolidation; pricing and promotional activities of
existing and new competitors, including non-traditional competitors; our
response to these actions; unexpected changes in product costs; the state of
the economy, including interest rates and the inflationary and deflationary
trends in certain commodities; the extent to which our customers exercise
caution in their purchasing behavior in response to economic conditions; the
number of shares outstanding; the success of our future growth plans; goodwill
impairment; volatility in our fuel margins; and our ability to generate sales
at desirable margins, as well as the success of our programs designed to
increase our identical sales without fuel. In addition, any delays in opening
new stores, or changes in the economic climate, could cause us to fall short of
our sales and earnings targets.&#160; Our
ability to increase identical supermarket sales could be adversely affected by
increased competition and sales shifts to other stores that we operate, as well
as increases in sales of our corporate brand products. Earnings and sales also
may be affected by climate change and adverse weather conditions, particularly
to the extent that hurricanes, tornadoes, floods, and other conditions disrupt
our operations or those of our suppliers; create shortages in the availability
or increases in the cost of products that we sell in our stores or materials
and ingredients we use in our manufacturing facilities; or raise the cost of
supplying energy to our various operations, including the cost of
transportation.&nbsp; Our guidance for LIFO is based on our forecast of cost
changes for products in our inventory. Our estimate of product cost changes
could be affected by general economic conditions, weather, availability of raw
materials and ingredients in the products that we sell and their packaging, and
other factors beyond our control. Our non-fuel operating margin guidance could
change if we are unable to pass on any cost increases, if our strategies fail
to deliver the cost savings contemplated, or if changes in the cost of our
inventory and the timing of those changes differ from our expectations.&#160; Our LIFO charge and the timing of our
recognition of LIFO expense will be affected by changes in product costs during
the year.&nbsp; Our fuel margins could fail to normalize at 11&#162; per gallon if
the pattern of rapid changes in fuel costs continues.&nbsp; Our capital
expenditures, and the number of projects that we complete, could vary from our
expectations if we are unsuccessful in acquiring suitable sites for new stores;
development costs vary from those budgeted; our logistics and technology or
store projects are not completed on budget or within the time frame projected;
or if current operating conditions fail to improve, or worsen.&#160; Square footage growth during the year is
dependent upon our ability to acquire desirable sites for construction of new
facilities, as well as the timing of completion of projects.&#160; Any change in tax laws, the regulations
related thereto, </font></p>

<body lang="EN-US">

<div style="font-family:Times New Roman;">

<p align="right" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:right;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">EXHIBIT
99.1</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">KROGER REPORTS FOURTH QUARTER AND FULL YEAR 2009 RESULTS</font></b></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">CINCINNATI,
Ohio, March&nbsp;9, 2010 &#151; The Kroger Co. (NYSE: KR) today reported total
sales, including fuel, increased 7.2% to $18.6 billion in the fourth quarter of
fiscal 2009 compared with $17.3 billion for the same period last year.&#160; Excluding fuel sales, in the fourth quarter
total sales increased 2.0% and identical supermarket sales increased 1.2% over
the prior year.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Net
earnings for the fourth quarter, which ended on January&nbsp;30, 2010, totaled
$255.4 million, or $0.39 per diluted share.&#160;
Net earnings in the same period last year were $349.2 million, or $0.53
per diluted share.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="left" style="font-weight:bold;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:normal;">&#147;The Kroger team delivered solid
fourth quarter results for both our customers and our shareholders during what
continues to be a difficult operating environment.&#160; We are strengthening Kroger&#146;s overall
competitive position by increasing the number of households that are loyal to
Kroger and earning a greater share of their business,&#148; said David B. Dillon,
Kroger&#146;s chairman and chief executive officer.</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Details
of Fourth Quarter Results</font></u></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Including Kroger&#146;s retail fuel operations, FIFO
gross margin (Table 1) was 22.48% of sales, a decrease of 214 basis points
compared to the fourth quarter last year.&#160;
Excluding retail fuel operations, FIFO gross margin decreased 112 basis
points.&#160; Supermarket selling gross margin
on non-fuel sales decreased 126 basis points.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">T</font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">he Company recorded a $1.3 million LIFO
charge during the quarter, a decrease of $39.6 million from the same period in
the prior year.&#160; Excluding retail fuel
operations, the LIFO charge decreased 25 basis points as a percent of sales
compared to the same period last year.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Including
Kroger&#146;s retail fuel operations, operating, general, and administrative
(OG&amp;A) costs were 16.98% of sales, a decrease of 73 basis points compared
to the fourth quarter last year.&nbsp; Excluding retail fuel operations,
OG&amp;A increased 10 basis points compared with the same period last year as a
result of higher health care and labor costs, and credit card fees.&#160; </font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<div style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><hr size="3" width="100%" noshade color="#010101" align="left"></div>

</div>
<!-- SEQ.=1,FOLIO='',FILE='C:\JMS\105938\10-5411-1\task3981463\5411-1-mm-01.htm',USER='105938',CD='Mar  9 10:20 2010' -->


<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">


<div style="font-family:Times New Roman;">

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">This
increase was partially offset by lower utility costs, improvements in labor
productivity and lower incentive pay.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Financial
Strategy</font></u></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Capital investment, excluding acquisitions and
purchases of leased facilities, totaled $458.9 </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">million for the fourth
quarter, compared with $434.0 million for the same period last year.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Net
total debt (Table 5) was $7.5 billion, a decrease of $217.5 million from a year
ago.&#160; On a rolling four-quarters basis,
Kroger&#146;s net total debt to EBITDA ratio, adjusted for the southern California
asset impairment charges in the third quarter, was 1.97 compared with 1.88
during the same period last year.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">During
the fourth quarter, Kroger repurchased 4.2 million shares of stock at an
average price of $21.08 per share for a total investment of $88.0 million.&#160; At the end of the quarter, $337.1 million
remained under the $1 billion stock repurchase program announced in January&nbsp;2008.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Fiscal Year 2009 Results</font></u></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">For
fiscal year 2009, total sales increased 0.8% to $76.7 billion compared with
fiscal 2008.&nbsp; Excluding fuel sales, total sales for fiscal 2009 increased
2.9%, and identical supermarket sales rose 2.1% compared with the prior fiscal
year.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Net
earnings for fiscal 2009 were $70.0 million, or $0.11 per diluted share.&#160; Current year results include the effect of
the southern California asset impairment charges in the third quarter.&#160; Excluding these items, net earnings for
fiscal 2009 would have been $1.12 billion, or $1.71 per diluted share (Table
6).</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Net
earnings in fiscal 2008 were $1.25 billion, or $1.89 per diluted share.&#160; Fiscal 2008 results include expenses for
damage and disruption caused by Hurricane Ike in the third quarter.&#160; Excluding these hurricane-related expenses,
fiscal year 2008 net earnings were $1.27 billion or $1.91 per diluted share
(Table 6).</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">During
2009, Kroger invested $2.15 billion in capital projects, excluding acquisitions
and purchases of leased facilities.&#160; The
Company repurchased 10.3 million shares of stock at an average price of $21.25
per share for a total investment of $218.3 million.&#160; Kroger also paid $237.6 million in cash
dividends.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<div style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><hr size="3" width="100%" noshade color="#010101" align="left"></div>

</div>
<!-- SEQ.=1,FOLIO='',FILE='C:\JMS\105938\10-5411-1\task3981463\5411-1-mm-01.htm',USER='105938',CD='Mar  9 10:20 2010' -->


<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">


<div>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="left" style="font-weight:bold;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:normal;">&#147;Throughout 2009, Kroger
successfully achieved identical sales growth, one of the key objectives of our
business model,&#148; Mr.&nbsp;Dillon said.&#160; &#147;Through
the efforts of all of our associates, we continue to widen the gap between
Kroger&#146;s identical sales growth trends and those of most of our
competitors.&#160; We believe this has
extremely positive implications for our associates, customers and shareholders both
now and as we grow our business.&#148;</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Fiscal
Year 2010 Guidance</font></u></b></p>

<p align="left" style="font-weight:bold;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:normal;">For fiscal year 2010, Kroger
anticipates identical supermarket sales growth, excluding fuel, of 2% to
3%.&nbsp; Net earnings are expected to range from $1.60 to $1.80 per diluted
share.&nbsp; Kroger&#146;s quarterly dividend enhances total shareholder return by
approximately 1.5% to 2.0%.</font></b></p>

<p align="left" style="font-weight:bold;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Kroger
believes several factors that influenced its business in the last half of 2009
will continue at least through the first half of 2010.&nbsp; Inflation or
deflation in product and operating costs, the competitive environment,
fluctuating fuel margins, and the pace of the economic recovery are uncertain
and cause Kroger to be cautious about its fiscal year 2010 forecast.&nbsp; We
expect trends in these areas to influence the Company&#146;s results throughout
fiscal year 2010.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="left" style="font-weight:bold;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:normal;">&#147;During a year that proved to be
extremely trying, Kroger successfully achieved positive identical sales growth,
increased the number of households loyal to Kroger stores, and generated strong
tonnage growth. In addition, we reduced debt, increased the dividend we pay
shareholders and prudently invested capital to keep our stores fresh and
innovative,&#148; Mr.&nbsp;Dillon said.&#160; &#147;Kroger&#146;s
strategy generates value in good times and bad.&#160;
We believe Kroger will continue to be in the best position to deliver
shareholder value now and as the economy improves.&#148;</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Kroger,
the nation&#146;s largest traditional grocery retailer, employs more than 334,000
associates who serve customers in 2,468 supermarkets and multi-department
stores in 31 states under two dozen local banner names including Kroger, City
Market, Dillons, Jay C, Food 4 Less, Fred Meyer, Fry&#146;s, King Soopers, QFC,
Ralphs and Smith&#146;s.&#160; The Company also
operates 777 convenience stores, 374 fine jewelry stores, 893 supermarket fuel
centers and 40 food processing plants in the U.S.&#160; Kroger, headquartered in Cincinnati, Ohio,
focuses </font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<div style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><hr size="3" width="100%" noshade color="#010101" align="left"></div>

</div>
<!-- SEQ.=1,FOLIO='',FILE='C:\JMS\105938\10-5411-1\task3981463\5411-1-mm-01.htm',USER='105938',CD='Mar  9 10:20 2010' -->


<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">


<div>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">its
charitable efforts on supporting hunger relief, health and wellness
initiatives, and local organizations in the communities it serves.&#160; For more information about Kroger, please
visit www.kroger.com.</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;"># # #</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Note:&#160; Fuel sales have historically had a low FIFO
gross margin rate and OG&amp;A rate as compared to corresponding rates on
non-fuel sales.&#160; As a result, Kroger
discloses such rates, both including and excluding the effect of retail fuel
operations.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">This press release contains certain forward-looking statements about
the future performance of the Company. These statements are based on management&#146;s
assumptions and beliefs in light of the information currently available to it.
Such statements are indicated by words such as &#147;anticipates,&#148; &#147;expected,&#148; &#147;believe,&#148;
and &#147;enhances.&#148; Increased competition, economic conditions, interest rates,
goodwill impairment, the success of programs designed to increase our identical
supermarket sales without fuel, and labor disputes, particularly as the Company
seeks to manage increases in health care and pension costs, could materially
affect our expected identical supermarket sales growth, earnings per share, and
earnings per share growth. Earnings per share and earnings per share growth
also will be affected by the number of shares outstanding and volatility in the
Company&#146;s fuel margins. Earnings and sales also may be affected by climate
change and adverse weather conditions, particularly to the extent that
hurricanes, tornadoes, floods, and other conditions disrupt our operations or
those of our suppliers; create shortages in the availability or increases in
the cost of products that we sell in our stores or materials and ingredients we
use in our manufacturing facilities; or raise the cost of supplying energy to
our various operations, including the cost of transportation.&nbsp; These
forward-looking statements are subject to uncertainties and other factors that
could cause actual results to differ materially. The extent to which our
quarterly dividend enhances shareholder return will depend on the continued
declaration of a quarterly dividend by our Board, and the amount of such
dividend, as well as the price at which our stock trades.&nbsp; We assume no
obligation to update the information contained herein. Please refer to Kroger&#146;s
reports and filings with the Securities and Exchange Commission for a further
discussion of these risks and uncertainties.</font></p>

Kroger&#146;s quarterly conference call with investors will be broadcast live online
at 10&nbsp;a.m. (ET) today at <i>www.kroger.com</i>
and <i>www.streetevents.com</i>.&#160; An on-demand replay of the webcast will be
available from approximately 1&nbsp;p.m. (ET) today through March&nbsp;19,
2010.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<div style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><hr size="1" width="25%" noshade color="black" align="left"></div>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Note: Certain prior-year
amounts have been reclassified to conform to current-year presentation.&#160; Certain per share amounts and percentages may
not sum due to rounding.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Note:&#160; The Company defines FIFO gross margin, as
described in the earnings release, as sales minus merchandise costs, including
advertising, warehousing and transportation, but excluding the Last-In
First-Out (LIFO) charge.&#160; This measure is
included to reflect trends in current cost of product.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Note:&#160; The Company defines selling gross margin, as
described in the earnings release related to the Company&#146;s supermarkets, as
gross margin before incurring expenses directly related to distributing and
merchandising the products on its store shelves.&#160; These expenses include advertising,
warehousing, transportation, and shrink.&#160;
Selling gross margin is a measure of how competitively the Company is
pricing the products it sells.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(a)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Merchandise
costs and operating, general and administrative expenses exclude depreciation
and amortization expense and rent expense which are included in separate
expense lines.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(b)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">LIFO charges of
$1.3 and $40.9 were recorded in the fourth quarter of 2009 and 2008,
respectively.&#160; For the year-to-date
period, LIFO charges of $49.0 and $195.9 were recorded for 2009 and 2008,
respectively.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(c)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">In the first
quarter of 2009, the Company adopted the amended standards for noncontrolling
interests in consolidated financial statements.&#160;
As a result, for those entities the Company consolidates but that are
not wholly-owned, Net Earnings Including Noncontrolling Interests includes the
entire amount of net earnings (loss) from those entities.&#160; The portion of those entities&#146; net earnings
(loss) not attributable to The Kroger Co. is then removed from Net Earnings
Including Noncontrolling Interests in order to determine Net Earnings
Attributable to The Kroger Co.&#160; These rules&nbsp;have
been retroactively applied to all periods presented, which changed income
statement line amounts, but did not change Net Earnings Attributable to The
Kroger Co. (Dollar amounts for prior periods previously presented as Net
Earnings, which are now presented as Net Earnings Attributable to The Kroger
Co., have not changed as a result of the amended standards for noncontrolling
interests in consolidated financial statements.)</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<div>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Table 2.</font></b></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">THE KROGER CO.</font></b></p>

<div style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><hr size="1" width="25%" noshade color="black" align="left"></div>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(a)&#160;&#160; Kroger defines a supermarket as identical when it has been open
without expansion or relocation for five full quarters.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(b)&#160;&#160; Kroger defines a supermarket as comparable when it has been open
for five full quarters, including expansions and relocations.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">


<div>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Table
5.&#160; Reconciliation of Total Debt to Net
Total Debt</font></b></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(in millions)</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(unaudited)</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Net total debt should not be considered an alternative
to any GAAP measure of performance or liquidity.&#160; Management believes net total debt is an
important measure of liquidity, and a primary component of measuring compliance
with the financial covenants under the Company&#146;s credit facility.&#160; Net total debt should be reviewed in
conjunction with Kroger&#146;s financial results reported in accordance with GAAP.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The following table provides a reconciliation of total
debt to net total debt and compares the balance in the fourth quarter of 2009
to the balance in the fourth quarter of 2008.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<table border="0" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0" width="100%" style="border-collapse:collapse;width:100.0%;">
 <tr>
  <td width="55%" valign="bottom" style="padding:0in 0in 0in 0in;width:55.5%;">
  <p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="1" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:1.0pt;font-weight:bold;">&nbsp;</font></b></p>
  </td>
  <td width="2%" valign="bottom" style="padding:0in 0in 0in 0in;width:2.5%;">
  <p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="1" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:1.0pt;font-weight:bold;">&nbsp;</font></b></p>

other GAAP measure of performance.&#160; These
items should not be reviewed in isolation or considered substitutes for the
Company&#146;s financial results as reported in accordance with GAAP.&#160; Due to the nature of these items, as further described

them in conjunction with the Company&#146;s financial results reported in accordance
with GAAP.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(a)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">After-tax
goodwill impairment charge ($1,112.7 pre-tax) relating to a Southern California
reporting unit.&#160; Most of the goodwill
impairment charge is non-deductible for tax purposes.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(b)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">After-tax asset impairment
charges ($24.1 pre-tax) relating to underperforming stores in a Southern
California reporting unit.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(c)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">After-tax charges ($25.0
pre-tax) relating to Hurricane Ike.</font></p>
